name:Z‚Äçh‚Äça‚Äço‚Äçc‚Äçh‚Äçu‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçb‚Äçe‚Äçi
info:Superior Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:21 Reviews
rating:3
posted:Posted April 5, 2024
msg:I can only say that I am basically satisfied. The hotel dinner restaurant is not well managed.

Service: I checked in around 18:40 in the evening, packed up and took the elderly and children to find food. The area is relatively remote, so we can only eat in the hotel restaurant. I was arranged to the 9th private room, which was only for individual guests. Because I was tired after a day and had a trip tomorrow, I wanted to eat something quickly and rest. I ordered the dishes around 19:35. I ordered a roasted tofu, a stir-fried broccoli, a pork vermicelli, and a portion of rice. Except for pork, I think they should all be quick dishes.
But I waited until around 20:20, and no dish was served. The people at the next table came later than us and ate. The children were hungry, and my husband kept standing at the door of the private room to urge him. His attitude was not too impatient, but the waiter kept driving him away, telling him not to urge him anymore, saying that the kitchen would not come, and they had no choice, and they had already urged him.
At 20:30, still no dish was served. I went to ask the waiter why, but the waiter was impatient and asked me to go back and wait. We didn't agree and argued with him. A girl who looked like a foreman came and explained that the dishes on the neighboring table were served quickly because they ordered a set meal, which was all prepared. We ordered a single dish, which had to be processed on the spot, so it was slow.
I think this is completely untenable.
First, we didn't order complex ingredients, which didn't require fine processing. Cutting the dishes that could be served on the menu that day should not have the problem of long-term temporary processing. I made these two vegetables at home in 10 minutes. I don't believe that the rice was cooked fresh, and no one told me. In the end, the pork vermicelli was not served on the table, and it was returned.
Second, if the hotel promotes pre-made set meals, why didn't we recommend it when ordering?
Third, even if the guests insisted on ordering on the spot and didn't order a set meal, why didn't they tell us in advance that it would take a long time to wait? What's more, it was already late when ordering dishes, which shows that the service awareness was terrible.
I don't know if this hotel has no requirements for service management, or if the waiters are eating from the same pot without performance system constraints. In short, in this era of competitive service, this low-level service attitude and service method really surprised me.

In other aspects, the hotel hardware, room configuration, breakfast, etc. are all acceptable. Just for the Qingming Festival holiday, the price of 500 per night is still cost-effective. Also, I can't see the sea at all in the hotel.
----------------------------------------
